 In the Akhand Jyoti temple of Ujjain, devotees see the miracle of Hanuman
 jahaan ek taraf mandir main jal rahi akhand jyoti ke darshan kar aate kaa diya jalaane bhar se sadhesati se mukti mil jaati he, vahiin anya manokamanaayon ke liye bhakt bajrangbali ko alag-alag prasad kaa bhoga lagaate hai

 anant aasthaa se shraddhalu pavanputra se vinati karte hai

 kehete hai lakshmana ko bachaane ke liye jab hanuman sanjivani lekar aa rahe the to lankini naam kii rakshasi ne unka rasta roak kar unhen jane se roka, jiske baad hanuman, lankini ko apane pairon ke neeche dabaakar aage bad gaye the
 In this temple, the same form of Mahavir is seen where Lankini still sits under the feet of Hanuman
 puure saaj shringaar ke saath bal brahmacharee kaa ye rup bada hi manamohak he

 haathon main bajuband, paanv main paajeb or kalai main kade pahane hue mahavir ke divya rup ke darshan maatr se bhakton ke sabhi ksht dur ho jate hai
 According to the name of the temple, the burning unbroken lamp here tells the devotees the story of the miracle of Bajrambali
 you to dekhne main ye mandir hanuman ke anya mandiron kii tarah hi he lekin mandir main saalon se jal rahe akhand diye main bajrangbali kii chamatkaari shaktiyaan samahit hai
 It is said that if the devotees troubled by the half-century come to this temple and see this unbroken lamp and burn a lamp of flour in the temple, then it does not take long to get rid of Saturn's wrath
 bhakt hanuman ji ko yahaan kai tarah ke prasad chadhaate hai
 It is said that devotees bring here through their wish offerings
 agar kisi ko jhagade, makadamon se chhutkaaraa chahie to ek nariyal ke arpan maatr se uske tamaam kashton kaa nivaaran ho jaataa he
 In the same way, the devotees who wish to have children, according to their power and devotion, resolve to offer 1, 2 or 5 kg of oil in the unbroken light
 chane-chirunji se prasann hone vaale hanuman ko yahaan visheshtaur se rot ke prasad kaa bhoga lagaaya jaataa he

 mandir main pratidin hone vaali aarti kaa gavaah banane ke liye badi sankhya main bhakton sailaab umadta he

 mangalvaar or shanivaar ko yahaan puja karne kaa vishesh mahatv he

 of Kashmir will be exploited
 kashmir main iske alaava hastshilp or anya kam pradooshan vaale udyogon kaa bhi vikaas kiya jayega

 confaderation of indian industry ke namit adhyaksh udai kotak ke mutabik sarkaar or udyog jagat ke majboot prayaason se rajya main growth rate or rojgaar ke avasaron ko badhaane main madad milegi
 There is also a lot of opportunity for development of hydroelectric projects and solar power in the state
 jammu-kashmir kii arthvyavastha abhi tak mukhya rup se kendriya anudaan par nirbhar karti thi, jiskaa yogadan yahaan ke kul rajasav ke aadhe se zyada hota he
 The state has seen a growth rate of 10 per cent in the last five years, but this is due to the base rate being much lower
 rajya kii arthvyavastha kheti or sevaaon par nirbhar he
 The major industries of the state are tourism, handicrafts, silk production, handlooms, horticulture, food processing and agriculture
 haalanki, rajya ke aarthik surveykshan se pataa chalata he ki sakal rajya gharelu utpaada kaa mahaj 0

 ) Usually after hearing the name of the jail, the goons of miscreants become breathless
 wo jail kii roti khaane se bachane kii jugat main lag jate hai, lekin ab aise din guzar gaye
 Now those days have come, when the convicts inside the jail have started getting health
 wo pehle se kahin zyada chust-durust or tandurust ho gaye hai
 The weight of many prisoners has increased from seven to fifteen kilos
 raipur ke central jail main jab kaidiyon kaa medical test hua to unki sehat dekh kar jail prashasan bhi sakate main aa gaya
 Seeing the flourishing color of the prisoners, the officials are saying that the jail has become a reform house, not a torture house
 raipur ke central jail main sajaa kaat rahe in kaidiyon kii tandoorusti dekhte hi ban rahi he
 Naresh, who is serving a seven-year sentence for cheating in the Central Jail, was only 60 kg when he was lodged in jail eight months ago
 lekin abhi saal bhar bhi nahin hua ki uskaa vajan 77 kilo tak pahunch gaya he
 The same situation is with Ravi and Manish
 ye donon kaidi aaajeevan karawas kii sajaa bhugat rahe hai
 Not only the King, out of the nearly three thousand prisoners lodged in the Central Jail, there are 1,435 such prisoners whose weight has increased by an average of seven to fifteen kilos
 in kaidiyon kaa sirf vajan hi nahin badha balki kai bimariyon se bhi unako chhutkaaraa mil gaya
 The appearance of many has changed
 kai kaa pet tak nikal aayaa he
 According to DIG KK Gupta of Raipur Central Jail, earlier the emphasis was on just feeding food to the inmates in the jail and not on the quality
 ab gunvattta ko mahatva diya jaataa he, saath hi khaane ke swaad par bhi
 According to him, all prisoners are getting calorie-rich food on time, better health facilities and many free facilities
 jail manual ke anusaar vidharadhin kaidico rojaanaa 1800 calories yukt or sajayaftaa kaidi ko 2100 calories yukt bhojan diya jaataa he
 Apart from this, tea and breakfast are available in the morning and evening
 tyoharon or rashtriya parvo par vishesh bhojan parosa jaataa he
 They are also subjected to physical labor to keep them healthy
 ruchi ke anusaar kaam diya jaataa he
 They are provided with food ranging from steam food to gas
 medical jaanch main saamne aayaa he kikul purush kaidiyon kii sankhya mense 48 fisadi kaidiyon kaa vajan saat se das kilo tak badha he
 Eight percent of prisoners have increased in weight by 15 kg
 14 fisadi kaidi jail main daakhil hone ke baad slim trim hue hai
 While 33% of the prisoners are fully fit and normal
 jiesti (maal or seva kar) abhi bhi puure desh ke logon ke liye ek badi uljhan bani hui he
 It has been almost 50 days since GST was implemented, but people are still in trouble as to how GST is implemented on different items
 bataa den ki jiesti 1 july, 2017 ko lagu kiya gaya tha
 Usually a consumer goes to a hotel or restaurant to eat and drink, then does not look at the bill carefully
 lekin jiesti lagu hone ke baad bhi aap yadi aisa nahin karte to sambhav he ki aapse zyada paisa vasula ja rahaa he
 There are still many restaurants that charge tax as per their choice
 bill par lagaae gaye tex kii jaanch karte samay in chijen kaa rakhen dhyaan
 1
 seva shulkkisi bhi restaraan main seva shulk kaa bhugtan karnaa anivaary nahin he
 The customer is entitled to refuse to pay the service fee
 ise sarkaar dwaara nahin lagaaya gaya he
 2
 restaraan main lagu jiesti daren kya he?vibhinn khaane ke outlet yaa restaraan main alag-alag jiesti daren hai
 For non-ac restaurants / non-alcoholic serving hotels, it is 12%
 -asi / alcohol-sevarat hotel ke liye, yah 18% he
 For 5-star hotels, this is 28%
 3
 What is SGST and CGST? Many consumers are confused between SGST and CGST
 esgsti rajya ke maal or seva kar ke liye he, jabaki sijisti kendriya maal or seva kar ke liye he
 It also means that half of the tax you pay goes to the state treasury while the other half goes to the central government treasury
 4
 Is the restaurant you are dining in eligible for GST charge? This may surprise you but not all restaurants and restaurants are in charge of GST
 gaiyr-panjikrut vyavsaayon ko jiesti par shulk lagane kii anumati nahin he
 It is registered to find out which restaurant you are eating at
